Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from scans made from Don Eyles's personal copy of Luminary 069. They were scanned at archive.org's Boston facility, and the scanning was sponsored by Onno Hommes. The code was transcribed from these scans by a team of volunteers who are referenced in the program comments. Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". In some cases, where similar code blocks exist in previously-transcribed AGC programs (primarily Luminary 99, from Apollo 11) those code blocks were used as a starting point and then corrected to agree with the Luminary 69 scans. The full scans are available at the Virtual AGC project's collection at archive.org, while more-convenient reduced-size (but reduced-quality) images are available at the main Virtual AGC website. Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 069 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-011
	19:02 NOV. 25,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

022264,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
022265,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
022266,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     The main source file for Luminary revision 069.
022267,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the original release
022268,000006:                                                                                                  ##              of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
022269,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10. The actual flown
022270,000008:                                                                                                  ##              version was Luminary 69 revision 2, which included a
022271,000009:                                                                                                  ##              newer lunar gravity model and only affected module 2.
022272,000010:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
022273,000011:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
022274,000012:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
022275,000013:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
022276,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 504-623
022277,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
022278,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
022279,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
022280,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2016-12-13 MAS  Created from Luminary 99.
022281,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2016-12-14 MAS  Updated from comment-proofed Luminary 99 version.
022282,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2016-01-16 HG   Transcribed
022283,000021:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-22 HG   Shift pseudo label +3 to column 2.
022284,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              Add missing operator INHINT
022285,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-23 HG   Fix operator CCS -> CA
022286,000024:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix value TENDEG .27... -> .027...
022287,000025:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand R22LEM42 -> R22LEM
022288,000026:                                                                                                  ##                                          GOXDSPF  -> GOXDSPFR
022289,000027:                                                                                                  ##                                          BIT13    -> BIT3
022290,000028:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand modifier WWPOS +6 -> WWPOS +4
022291,000029:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix statement CA FLAGWRD2 -> CS FLAGWRD0
022292,000030:                                                                                                  ##                                            EXTEND      -> CCS A
022293,000031:                                                                                                  ##                                            BZF NOTP20  -> TC  NOTP20
022294,000032:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-27 RSB  Proofed comment text using octopus/prooferComments
022295,000033:                                                                                                  ##                              and fixed errors found.
022296,000034:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-28 RSB  WTIH -> WITH.
022297,000035:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-13 RSB  Comment-text fixes noted in proofing Luminary 116.
022298,000036:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-16 RSB  Comment-text fixes identified in 5-way
022299,000037:                                                                                                  ##                              side-by-side diff of Luminary 69/99/116/131/210.
022300,000038:

022303,000041: 
022304,000042:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
022305,000043:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022306,000044:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022307,000045:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022308,000046:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022309,000047: 
022310,000048:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
022311,000049:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
022312,000050:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
022313,000051:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
022314,000052:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022315,000053: 
022316,000054:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
022317,000055:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022318,000056:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
022319,000057:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
022320,000058:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
022321,000059:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
022322,000060:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
022323,000061:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
022324,000062:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
022325,000063:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
022326,000064:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
022327,000065:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
022328,000066:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022329,000067:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022330,000068:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022331,000069:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022332,000070:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
022333,000071:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022334,000072:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
022335,000073:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022336,000074:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022337,000075:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
022338,000076:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022339,000077:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
022340,000078: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
022341,000079: 
022342,000080: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
022343,000081: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
022344,000082: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
022345,000083: 
022346,000084: 24,2022  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022347,000085: 24,2022                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
022348,000086: 24,2022  24,2022               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
022349,000087: 24,2022           05327        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG

022777,000515:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022778,000516:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022779,000517:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022780,000518:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022781,000519:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022782,000520: 
022783,000521:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022784,000522:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022785,000523:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022786,000524:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022787,000525:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022788,000526:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022789,000527:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022790,000528:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022791,000529:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022792,000530:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022793,000531:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022794,000532:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022795,000533:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022796,000534:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022797,000535:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022798,000536:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022799,000537:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022800,000538:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022801,000539:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET

022852,000590:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022853,000591:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022854,000592:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022855,000593:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022856,000594:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022857,000595: 
022858,000596:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022859,000597:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022860,000598:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022861,000599:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022862,000600:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
022863,000601:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022864,000602:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
022865,000603:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
022866,000604:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
022867,000605:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022868,000606:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA

023053,000791:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
023054,000792:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023055,000793:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023056,000794:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023057,000795:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023058,000796: 
023059,000797:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
023060,000798:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
023061,000799:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023062,000800:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023063,000801:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
023064,000802:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
023065,000803:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
023066,000804:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
023067,000805:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
023068,000806:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
023069,000807:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
023070,000808:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
023071,000809:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
023072,000810:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023073,000811:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
023074,000812:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
023075,000813:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
023076,000814:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023077,000815:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023078,000816:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023079,000817:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
023080,000818:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023081,000819:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
023082,000820:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
023083,000821:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023084,000822: 24,2721  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023085,000823: 24,2721                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
023086,000824: 24,2721           32341        R21LEM             CAF      MAXTRIES                              #  ALLOW 60 PASSES (APPROX 45 SECS.) TO
023087,000825: 24,2722           55114                           TS       DESCOUNT                              #  DESIGNATE AND LOCKON

023164,000902:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM

023166,000904:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2

023169,000907: 
023170,000908:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR

023234,000972:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
023235,000973:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023236,000974:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023237,000975:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
023238,000976:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023239,000977: 
023240,000978:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
023241,000979:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
023242,000980:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
023243,000981:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
023244,000982:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
023245,000983:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
023246,000984:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
023247,000985:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
023248,000986:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023249,000987:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
023250,000988:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
023251,000989:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
023252,000990:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023253,000991:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
023254,000992:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
023255,000993:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
023256,000994:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023257,000995:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023258,000996:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
023259,000997:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
023260,000998:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023261,000999:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
023262,001000:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023263,001001:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
023264,001002: 24,3100  E7,1731                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
023265,001003: 24,3100                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
023266,001004: 24,3100           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
023267,001005: 24,3101           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
023268,001006: 24,3102           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
023269,001007: 24,3103           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
023270,001008: 24,3104           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
023271,001009: 24,3105           55731                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
023272,001010: 24,3106           55732                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
023273,001011: 24,3107           55733                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

023338,001076:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
023339,001077:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

023531,001269:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023532,001270: 
023533,001271:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023534,001272:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023535,001273:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023536,001274:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023537,001275:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023538,001276:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023539,001277:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023540,001278:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023541,001279:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023542,001280:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023543,001281:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023544,001282:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023545,001283:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023546,001284:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023547,001285:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023548,001286: 
023549,001287:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023550,001288:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)

023555,001293:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023556,001294:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).

023611,001349:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023612,001350: 
023613,001351:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023614,001352:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023615,001353:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023616,001354:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023617,001355:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023618,001356:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023619,001357:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023620,001358:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023621,001359:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023622,001360:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023623,001361:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023624,001362:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023625,001363:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023626,001364:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023627,001365:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023628,001366:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023629,001367:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023630,001368:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023631,001369:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023632,001370:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL

023682,001420:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
023683,001421: 
023684,001422:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023685,001423: 
023686,001424:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023687,001425:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023688,001426:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023689,001427:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023690,001428:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023691,001429:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023692,001430:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023693,001431:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023694,001432:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023695,001433:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023696,001434:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023697,001435:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023698,001436: 
023699,001437:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023700,001438:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
023701,001439:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023702,001440: 
023703,001441:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023704,001442:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023705,001443: 
023706,001444:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023707,001445: 
023708,001446:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023709,001447:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023710,001448: 
023711,001449:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023712,001450: 
023713,001451:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023714,001452: 
023715,001453: 24,3151                                           BANK     24                                    
023716,001454: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023717,001455: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023718,001456: 
023719,001457: 25,2062  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023720,001458: 25,2062                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023721,001459: 25,2062           02071        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023722,001460: 25,2063           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023723,001461: 25,2064           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
023724,001462: 25,2065           44753                           CS       BIT1

023730,001468:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023731,001469: 
023732,001470:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023733,001471:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023734,001472:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023735,001473:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023736,001474:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023737,001475:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
023738,001476:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023739,001477:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023740,001478:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023741,001479:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023742,001480:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023743,001481:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023744,001482:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023745,001483:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023746,001484:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023747,001485:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023748,001486: 
023749,001487:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023750,001488:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023751,001489:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023752,001490: 
023753,001491:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023754,001492: 
023755,001493:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023756,001494:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023757,001495: 
023758,001496:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
023759,001497: 
023760,001498:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
023761,001499: 
023762,001500: 25,2071           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
023763,001501: 25,2072           23315                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
023764,001502: 25,2073           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
023765,001503: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
023766,001504: 25,2075           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
023767,001505: 25,2076           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
023768,001506: 25,2077           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
023769,001507: 
023770,001508: 25,2100           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
023771,001509: 25,2101           54035                           TS       CDUT                                  
023772,001510: 25,2102           54036                           TS       CDUS                                  
023773,001511: 25,2103           44753                           CS       ONE                                   #  REMOVE ZEROING BIT.
023774,001512: 25,2104           00006                           EXTEND

023776,001514: 25,2106           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
023777,001515: 25,2107           01750                           DEC      1000       B-14                       #  RESET FAIL INHIBIT IN 10 SECS - D.281
023778,001516: 
023779,001517: 25,2110           44737                           CS       BIT13                                 #  REMOVE ZEROING IN PROCESS BIT.
023780,001518:

Page 539 

023782,001520: 25,2111           70110                           MASK     RADMODES

023804,001542:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
023805,001543:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023806,001544:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023807,001545:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
023808,001546:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
023809,001547:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
023810,001548:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
023811,001549:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
023812,001550:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
023813,001551:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
023814,001552:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
023815,001553:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
023816,001554:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
023817,001555:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
023818,001556:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
023819,001557:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
023820,001558:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
023821,001559:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
023822,001560:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
023823,001561:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023824,001562:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
023825,001563:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
023826,001564:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
023827,001565:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
023828,001566: 
023829,001567:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023830,001568:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
023831,001569:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
023832,001570: 
023833,001571:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023834,001572:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023835,001573: 
023836,001574:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023837,001575:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
023838,001576: 
023839,001577:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023840,001578:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023841,001579: 
023842,001580:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE

023893,001631:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023894,001632: 
023895,001633:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023896,001634:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
023897,001635:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023898,001636:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023899,001637:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023900,001638:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023901,001639:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023902,001640:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023903,001641:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023904,001642:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023905,001643:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023906,001644:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023907,001645:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
023908,001646:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023909,001647:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023910,001648:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
023911,001649:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023912,001650:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023913,001651:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
023914,001652:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023915,001653: 
023916,001654:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023917,001655:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023918,001656:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023919,001657:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023920,001658:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
023921,001659: 
023922,001660:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023923,001661:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023924,001662:

023926,001664:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)

023987,001725:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023988,001726: 
023989,001727:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023990,001728:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023991,001729:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
023992,001730:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023993,001731:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
023994,001732:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
023995,001733:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023996,001734:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023997,001735:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
023998,001736:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023999,001737:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
024000,001738:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
024001,001739:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
024002,001740:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
024003,001741:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
024004,001742: 
024005,001743:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
024006,001744:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
024007,001745:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
024008,001746:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
024009,001747:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
024010,001748:

024012,001750:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES

024015,001753:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT

024076,001814:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
024077,001815: 
024078,001816:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024079,001817:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
024080,001818:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
024081,001819:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
024082,001820:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
024083,001821:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
024084,001822:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
024085,001823:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
024086,001824:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
024087,001825:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
024088,001826:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
024089,001827:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
024090,001828:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
024091,001829:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024092,001830: 
024093,001831:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024094,001832:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
024095,001833:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

024182,001920:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
024183,001921: 
024184,001922:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024185,001923:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
024186,001924:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
024187,001925:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
024188,001926:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
024189,001927:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
024190,001928:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
024191,001929:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
024192,001930:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
024193,001931:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
024194,001932:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
024195,001933:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
024196,001934:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
024197,001935:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
024198,001936:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
024199,001937:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
024200,001938:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
024201,001939:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
024202,001940:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
024203,001941:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
024204,001942:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
024205,001943:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
024206,001944:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
024207,001945: 
024208,001946:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024209,001947:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
024210,001948:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
024211,001949:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024212,001950:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024213,001951: 
024214,001952:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024215,001953:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
024216,001954: 
024217,001955:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024218,001956:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
024219,001957:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
024220,001958: 
024221,001959:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024222,001960:                                                                                                  #     NONE
024223,001961: 
024224,001962:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024225,001963: 
024226,001964:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
024227,001965:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
024228,001966:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
024229,001967: 
024230,001968: 25,2373           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
024231,001969: 25,2374           01113                                    DESRET

024236,001974: 25,2400           45175                           VLOAD    CALL                                  #  LOAD VECTOR AND CALL TRANSFORMATION
024237,001975: 25,2401           01102                                    RRTARGET                              
024238,001976: 25,2402           47575                                    *SMNB*

024268,002006:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
024269,002007: 
024270,002008:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
024271,002009:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
024272,002010:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024273,002011:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
024274,002012:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
024275,002013:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024276,002014:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
024277,002015:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
024278,002016:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
024279,002017:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
024280,002018:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
024281,002019:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
024282,002020:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
024283,002021:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
024284,002022:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
024285,002023:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
024286,002024:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
024287,002025:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
024288,002026:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
024289,002027:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
024290,002028:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024291,002029: 
024292,002030:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024293,002031:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
024294,002032: 
024295,002033:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024296,002034:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
024297,002035: 
024298,002036:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024299,002037:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR, WAITLIST
024300,002038: 
024301,002039:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024302,002040:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES
024303,002041: 
024304,002042:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024305,002043: 
024306,002044:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+3 OF CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM)
024307,002045:                                                                                                  #  L+2 OF CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESNB)
024308,002046:
