024439,002177:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024440,002178: 
024441,002179:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024442,002180:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024443,002181:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024444,002182:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024445,002183:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024446,002184:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024447,002185:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024448,002186:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024449,002187:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024450,002188:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024451,002189:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024452,002190:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024453,002191:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024454,002192:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024455,002193:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024456,002194:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024457,002195:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024458,002196:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024459,002197:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024460,002198:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024461,002199:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024462,002200:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024463,002201:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024464,002202:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024465,002203:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024466,002204:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024467,002205: 
024468,002206:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024469,002207:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024470,002208:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024471,002209:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024472,002210: 
024473,002211:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024474,002212:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024475,002213: 
024476,002214:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024477,002215:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024478,002216: 
024479,002217:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024480,002218: 
024481,002219:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024482,002220:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024483,002221: 
024484,002222:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024485,002223:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024486,002224:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024487,002225: 
024488,002226: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES                              
024489,002227:

Page 558 

024535,002273:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024536,002274: 
024537,002275:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024538,002276:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024539,002277:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024540,002278:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024541,002279:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024542,002280:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024543,002281:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024544,002282:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024545,002283:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024546,002284:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE
024547,002285:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024548,002286:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024549,002287:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE
024550,002288:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024551,002289:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024552,002290:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024553,002291:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024554,002292:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024555,002293:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024556,002294:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024557,002295:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024558,002296:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024559,002297:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024560,002298:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024561,002299:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024562,002300:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024563,002301:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024564,002302:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024565,002303:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024566,002304:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024567,002305:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024568,002306:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024569,002307:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024570,002308:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024571,002309:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024572,002310:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024573,002311:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024574,002312:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024575,002313: 
024576,002314:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024577,002315:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024578,002316: 
024579,002317:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024580,002318:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024581,002319:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024582,002320: 
024583,002321:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024584,002322:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
024585,002323:

Page 559 

024587,002325:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024588,002326:                                                                                                  #  NONE

024590,002328:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE

025366,003104:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025367,003105:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025368,003106: 
025369,003107: 
025370,003108:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025371,003109: 
025372,003110:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025373,003111:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025374,003112:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025375,003113: 
025376,003114:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025377,003115: 
025378,003116: 
025379,003117:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025380,003118: 
025381,003119: 
025382,003120:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025383,003121: 
025384,003122:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
025385,003123:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025386,003124:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025387,003125:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025388,003126:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025389,003127: 
025390,003128: 
025391,003129:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025392,003130: 
025393,003131:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025394,003132:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025395,003133: 
025396,003134: 
025397,003135:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025398,003136:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025399,003137: 
025400,003138: 
025401,003139:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025402,003140:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025403,003141: 
025404,003142:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025405,003143: 
025406,003144:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025407,003145:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025408,003146:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025409,003147:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
025410,003148:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
025411,003149: 
025412,003150: 
025413,003151:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025414,003152: 
025415,003153:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:
025416,003154:

Page 580 

025418,003156:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
025419,003157:                                                                                                  #      2)RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
025420,003158:

025422,003160:

025604,003342:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
025605,003343:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
025606,003344:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
025607,003345: 
025608,003346:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025609,003347: 
025610,003348:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
025611,003349:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
025612,003350:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
025613,003351: 
025614,003352:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025615,003353:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
025616,003354:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
025617,003355:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
025618,003356:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
025619,003357:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
025620,003358:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
025621,003359: 
025622,003360: 
025623,003361:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025624,003362:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
025625,003363:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
025626,003364: 
025627,003365:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025628,003366:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025629,003367:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025630,003368:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025631,003369:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025632,003370:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025633,003371: 
025634,003372: 
025635,003373:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025636,003374:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025637,003375:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025638,003376:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025639,003377:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025640,003378:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
025641,003379:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
025642,003380:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
025643,003381:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
025644,003382:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
025645,003383:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
025646,003384:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
025647,003385:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
025648,003386:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
025649,003387:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025650,003388: 
025651,003389:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025652,003390:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
025653,003391:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

026043,003781: 26,3141           77650        RENDEND            GOTO                                           
026044,003782: 26,3142           50614                                    R22LEM93                              
026045,003783:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026046,003784: 
026047,003785:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
026048,003786:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
026049,003787:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
026050,003788: 
026051,003789:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026052,003790:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
026053,003791:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
026054,003792: 
026055,003793:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026056,003794:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026057,003795:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026058,003796:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026059,003797:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026060,003798:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026061,003799: 
026062,003800:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED

026270,004008:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
026271,004009:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
026272,004010: 
026273,004011: 
026274,004012:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026275,004013: 
026276,004014:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026277,004015:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026278,004016:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026279,004017:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026280,004018: 
026281,004019: 
026282,004020:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026283,004021: 
026284,004022: 
026285,004023:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026286,004024: 
026287,004025:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026288,004026:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026289,004027:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026290,004028:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026291,004029:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026292,004030: 
026293,004031: 
026294,004032:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -  TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026295,004033: 
026296,004034: 
026297,004035:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026298,004036: 
026299,004037:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026300,004038:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026301,004039:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026302,004040: 
026303,004041:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026304,004042:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026305,004043:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026306,004044:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026307,004045: 
026308,004046:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026309,004047:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026310,004048:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026311,004049:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026312,004050:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026313,004051: 
026314,004052: 26,3405                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
026315,004053: 26,3405           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO

026318,004056: 26,3410           00006                           EXTEND

026588,004326:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29  (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
026589,004327:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2       BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
026590,004328: 
026591,004329: 
026592,004330:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
026593,004331: 
026594,004332:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
026595,004333:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
026596,004334:                                                                                                  #  THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
026597,004335:                                                                                                  #  THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
026598,004336:                                                                                                  #  DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
026599,004337:                                                                                                  #  INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
026600,004338: 
026601,004339:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
026602,004340: 
026603,004341: 
026604,004342:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
026605,004343: 
026606,004344:                                                                                                  #  REMODE   RRTONLY
026607,004345:                                                                                                  #  UNIT     MPACVBUF
026608,004346:                                                                                                  #  QUICTRIG AX*SR*T
026609,004347:                                                                                                  #  SPSIN    SPCOS
026610,004348:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR RROUT
026611,004349:                                                                                                  #  RRRDOT   RRRANGE
026612,004350: 
026613,004351: 
026614,004352:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
026615,004353: 
026616,004354: 
026617,004355:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
026618,004356: 
026619,004357:                                                                                                  #  RM       RDOTM                  (RAW)
026620,004358:                                                                                                  #  AIG      AMG
026621,004359:                                                                                                  #  AOG      TRKMKCNT               TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
026622,004360:                                                                                                  #  TANGNB   TANGNB +1              OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
026623,004361:                                                                                                  #  MKTIME
026624,004362:

Page 606 

026626,004364: 
026627,004365:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
026628,004366: 
026629,004367:                                                                                                  #  NOR29FLG READRFLG               (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START)  (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
026630,004368:                                                                                                  #  PIPTIME  RADMODES (BIT 10)      (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
026631,004369:                                                                                                  #  R(CSM)   V(CSM)
026632,004370:                                                                                                  #  R        V                      (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
026633,004371: 
026634,004372: 
026635,004373:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
026636,004374: 
026637,004375:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 10)
026638,004376:                                                                                                  #  LOSSM    LOSVDT/4       (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
026639,004377:                                                                                                  #  SAVECDUT OLDESFLG       (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
026640,004378:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG READRFLG
026641,004379: 
026642,004380: 
026643,004381:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
026644,004382: 
026645,004383: 
026646,004384:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
026647,004385: 
026648,004386:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE;  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
026649,004387:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
026650,004388:                                                                                                  #  RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
026651,004389: 
026652,004390: 
026653,004391: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
026654,004392: 33,2000                                           SETLOC   R29/SERV                              
026655,004393: 33,2000                                           BANK                                           
026656,004394: 
026657,004395: 33,2045                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
026658,004396: 
026659,004397: 33,2045     5014               NR29&RDR           EQUALS   EBANK5                                
026660,004398:

Page 607 

026662,004400:                                                                                                  #  SERVICER COMES TO R29 FROM "R29?" IF NOR29FLG, READRFLG, RRREMODE, RRCDUZRO, RRREPOS, AND DISPLAY-INERTIAL-DATA
026663,004401:                                                                                                  #  ARE ALL RESET, AND THE RR IS IN LGC MODE (OFTEN CONFUSINGLY CALLED AUTO MODE).
026664,004402: 
026665,004403: 33,2045           40110        R29                CS       RADMODES                              
026666,004404: 33,2046           74742                           MASK     BIT10                                 
026667,004405: 33,2047           00006                           EXTEND                                         
026668,004406: 33,2050           12123                           BZF      R29.LOS                               #  BRANCH IF DESIGNATION IS ALREADY ON.
026669,004407: 
026670,004408: 33,2051           00004                           INHINT                                         
026671,004409: 33,2052           26110                           ADS      RADMODES                              #  SHOW THAT DESIGNATION IS NOW ON.
026672,004410: 33,2053           44736                           CS       BIT14                                 
026673,004411: 33,2054           00006                           EXTEND                                         
026674,004412: 33,2055           03012                           WAND     CHAN12                                #  REMOVE RR TRACK ENABLE DISCRETE.
026675,004413: 33,2056           44740                           CS       LOSCMBIT                              
026676,004414: 33,2057           70076                           MASK     FLAGWRD2                              
026677,004415: 33,2060           54076                           TS       FLAGWRD2                              #  CLEAR LOSCMFLG TO SHOW DES. LOOP IS OFF.
026678,004416: 33,2061           44753                           CS       OLDESBIT                              
026679,004417: 33,2062           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 
026680,004418: 33,2063           54074                           TS       STATE                                 #  SHOW THAT DES. LOOP IS NOT REQUESTED.
026681,004419: 33,2064           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
026682,004420: 33,2065           52156                           CADR     SETRRECR                              #  ENABLE RR ERROR COUNTERS.
026683,004421: 33,2066           34740                           CA       BIT12                                 
026684,004422: 33,2067           70110                           MASK     RADMODES                              
026685,004423: 33,2070           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  TEST RR MODE BIT.
026686,004424: 33,2071           12104                           TCF      SETPRPOS                              #  MODE 2.
026687,004425: 
026688,004426: 33,2072           35031                           CA       PRIO21                                #  MODE 1; MUST REMODE.
026689,004427: 33,2073           05072                           TC       NOVAC                                 
026690,004428: 33,2074  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
026691,004429: 33,2074           02113 66067                     2CADR    R29REM0J                              #  NEEDS OWN JOB TO RADSTALL IN.
026692,004430: 
026693,004431: 33,2076           44742                           CS       BIT10                                 
026694,004432: 33,2077           70110                           MASK     RADMODES                              #  CLEAR DESIGNATE FLAG IN RADMODES
026695,004433: 33,2100           54110                           TS       RADMODES                              #  BEFORE CALLING REMODE
026696,004434: 33,2101           34736                           CA       BIT14                                 
026697,004435: 33,2102           26110                           ADS      RADMODES                              #   SHOW THAT REMODING IS ON.
026698,004436: 33,2103           12623                           TCF      NOR29NOW                              #  CONTINUE SERVICER FUNCTIONS.
026699,004437: 
026700,004438: 33,2104           34753        SETPRPOS           CA       ONE                                   
026701,004439: 33,2105           05203                           TC       WAITLIST                              
026702,004440: 33,2106  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
026703,004441: 33,2106           03601 52067                     2CADR    PREPOS29                              #  TASK TO SET TRUNNION ANGLE TO -180 DEG.
026704,004442: 
026705,004443: 33,2110           34741                           CA       BIT11                                 
026706,004444: 33,2111           26110                           ADS      RADMODES                              #  SHOW THAT REPOSITIONING IS ON.
026707,004445: 33,2112           12623                           TCF      NOR29NOW                              
026708,004446:

Page 608 

026710,004448:                                                                                                  #  FORCE RENDEZVOUS RADAR INTO MODE 2.
026711,004449: 
026712,004450: 33,2113           34753        R29REM0J           CA       ONE                                   
026713,004451: 33,2114           05203                           TC       WAITLIST                              
026714,004452: 33,2115  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
026715,004453: 33,2115           02171 52067                     2CADR    REMODE                                #  REMODE MUST RUN AS A TASK.
026716,004454: 33,2117           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              #  WAIT FOR END OF REMODING.
026717,004455: 33,2120           17667                           CADR     RADSTALL                              
026718,004456: 
026719,004457: 33,2121           15155                           TCF      ENDOFJOB                              #  BAD EXIT CAN'T HAPPEN.
026720,004458: 33,2122           15155                           TCF      ENDOFJOB                              
026721,004459: 
026722,004460:                                                                                                  #  TASK TO PREPOSITION THE RR TRUNNION ANGLE TO -180 DEG.
026723,004461: 
026724,004462: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   R29S1                                 
026725,004463: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
026726,004464:

026755,004493:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG=0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN

026830,004568:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
026831,004569: 
026832,004570:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
026833,004571:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
026834,004572:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
026835,004573:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
026836,004574:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
026837,004575: 
026838,004576:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
026839,004577:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
026840,004578: 
026841,004579: 32,2545                                           BANK     32                                    
026842,004580: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
026843,004581: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
026844,004582: 
026845,004583: 32,2545                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
026846,004584: 32,2545  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
026847,004585: 
026848,004586: 32,2545           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
026849,004587: 32,2546           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
026850,004588: 32,2547           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
026851,004589: 
026852,004590: 32,2550           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
026853,004591: 32,2551           54002                           TS       Q                                     
026854,004592: 32,2552           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
026855,004593: 32,2553           12561                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
026856,004594: 
026857,004595: 32,2554           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
026858,004596: 32,2555           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026859,004597: 32,2556           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
026860,004598: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026861,004599: 32,2560           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
026862,004600: 
026863,004601: 32,2561           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
026864,004602: 32,2562           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026865,004603: 32,2563           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
026866,004604: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
026867,004605: 32,2565           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
026868,004606: 32,2566           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
026869,004607: 32,2567           12575                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
026870,004608: 
026871,004609: 32,2570           00006                           EXTEND                                         
026872,004610: 32,2571           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026873,004611: 32,2572           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
026874,004612: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026875,004613: 32,2574           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
026876,004614: 
026877,004615: 32,2575           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
026878,004616: 32,2576           12550                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
026879,004617:

Page 612 

026881,004619:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
026882,004620: 
026883,004621: 32,2577           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         
026884,004622: 32,2600           52155                           DXCH     MPAC                                  
026885,004623: 32,2601           32770                           CA       R29FXLOC                              #  = ADRES INTB15+ -34D
026886,004624: 32,2602           54120                           TS       FIXLOC

026888,004626: 32,2604           01023                           CADR     UNIT                                  #  SQUARED, BORROW UNITIZING ROUTINE.
026889,004627: 32,2605           07531                           TC       MPACVBUF                              #  MOVE UNIT(LOS) TO AX*SR*T ARG AREA.
026890,004628: 
026891,004629: 32,2606           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
026892,004630: 32,2607           12611                           TCF      +2                                    
026893,004631: 32,2610           12625                           TCF      GOTANGLS                              #  GET CDU ANGLES ONLY AFTER 1ST PASS.
026894,004632: 32,2611           00004                           INHINT                                         #  ENSURE CONSISTENT CDU READINGS.
026895,004633: 32,2612           00006                           EXTEND

026898,004636: 32,2615           30033                           CA       CDUY

026904,004642: 32,2623           04616                           TC       BANKCALL

026908,004646: 32,2626           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
026909,004647: 32,2627           47601                           CADR     AX*SR*T                               #  TRANSFORM UNIT LOS TO NB AXES (ULOSNB).
026910,004648:

026914,004652:

026916,004654:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTE COSINE OF THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE PRESENT LOS AND THE RR BORESIGHT VECTOR, AND SET THE SELFTRACK ENABLE IF
026917,004655:                                                                                                  #  THE COSINE IS APPROXIMATELY COS(.5 DEG) OR GREATER (I.E. SMALLER ANGLE).
